name:g‚Äça‚Äçr‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçc‚Äçe‚Äç_‚Äçg‚Äça‚Äço
info:Business 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in October 2023

info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 4, 2023
msg:The hotel is themed on health preservation, and the details of health preservation are everywhere. There is free health tea at the entrance. There is a stone mat in the room, which can relax the feet and activate blood circulation. It is also in the shape of yin and yang fish. There are also herbal pillows to choose from. The hotel has a gym and a swimming pool, which is very convenient to go up and down in a building.
In addition to the hardware, the software service is also in place: the service staff are very polite, patient, and never tired of it. Especially the room service staff on my floor. When you check in, you can scan the code to get a gift. I applied and went downstairs to swim. When I came back, my husband said that the room service staff had come. But you have to scan a verification code. I was not there and could not scan it. They came back later. I was still thinking: How long is later? They knocked on the door and sent it to me. They were really thoughtful.
This hotel also pays special attention to the experience of guests. When I checked out, the front desk asked me if I had any suggestions. I said that I saw free laundry when I checked in, but when I wanted to wash it, the feedback was that the washed clothes should be returned before 12 o'clock, so I didn't dare to wash it. Because I was afraid that waiting for the clothes would delay the check-out. I thought if everyone only stayed for one day, then this free service would not be available?
I just gave feedback to the front desk and didn't have any expectations. Unexpectedly, the front desk immediately apologized and said that they were indeed not considerate of the time. In the afternoon, I received a call from the hotel to express sincere apologies and hope that I can stay in their hotel next time.
I think I will definitely stay there next time I go to Shijiazhuang. Not only was the experience very good, but I just asked a question, and I didn't expect the hotel to take it so seriously.
